3551     * Generate a sentence from this FakeLanguageGen that fits in the given length limit, using the given seed as a
3552     * long. The sentence's length in words will be between minWords and maxWords, both inclusive, unless it would
3553     * exceed maxChars, in which case it is truncated. It will put one of the punctuation Strings from
3554     * {@code midPunctuation} between two words (before the space) at a frequency of {@code midPunctuationFrequency}
3555     * (between 0 and 1), and will end the sentence with one String chosen from {@code endPunctuation}.
3556     *
3557     * @param seed                    the seed, as a long, for the randomized string building
3558     * @param minWords                an int for the minimum number of words in a sentence; should be at least 1
3559     * @param maxWords                an int for the maximum number of words in a sentence; should be at least equal to minWords
3560     * @param midPunctuation          a String array where each element is a comma, semicolon, or the like that goes before a
3561     *                                space in the middle of a sentence
3562     * @param endPunctuation          a String array where each element is a period, question mark, or the like that goes at
3563     *                                the very end of a sentence
3564     * @param midPunctuationFrequency a double between 0.0 and 1.0 that determines how often Strings from
3565     *                                midPunctuation should be inserted before spaces
3566     * @param maxChars                the longest string length this can produce; should be at least {@code 6 * minWords}
3567     * @return a sentence in the fake language as a String
3568     */
3569    public String sentence(long seed, int minWords, int maxWords, String[] midPunctuation, String[] endPunctuation,
3570                           double midPunctuationFrequency, int maxChars) {

3575    /**
3576     * Generate a sentence from this FakeLanguageGen using the given RNG that fits in the given length limit. The
3577     * sentence's length in words will be between minWords and maxWords, both inclusive, unless it would exceed
3578     * maxChars, in which case it is truncated. It will put one of the punctuation Strings from {@code midPunctuation}
3579     * between two words (before the space) at a frequency of {@code midPunctuationFrequency} (between 0 and 1), and
3580     * will end the sentence with one String chosen from {@code endPunctuation}.
3581     *
3582     * @param rng                     the RNG to use for the randomized string building
3583     * @param minWords                an int for the minimum number of words in a sentence; should be at least 1
3584     * @param maxWords                an int for the maximum number of words in a sentence; should be at least equal to minWords
3585     * @param midPunctuation          a String array where each element is a comma, semicolon, or the like that goes before a
3586     *                                space in the middle of a sentence
3587     * @param endPunctuation          a String array where each element is a period, question mark, or the like that goes at
3588     *                                the very end of a sentence
3589     * @param midPunctuationFrequency a double between 0.0 and 1.0 that determines how often Strings from
3590     *                                midPunctuation should be inserted before spaces
3591     * @param maxChars                the longest string length this can produce; should be at least {@code 6 * minWords}
3592     * @return a sentence in the fake language as a String
3593     */
3594    public String sentence(IRNG rng, int minWords, int maxWords, String[] midPunctuation, String[] endPunctuation,
3595                           double midPunctuationFrequency, int maxChars) {
3596        if(maxChars < 0)
3597            return sentence(rng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation, midPunctuationFrequency);
3598        if (minWords < 1)
3599            minWords = 1;
3600        if (minWords > maxWords)
3601            maxWords = minWords;
3602        if (midPunctuationFrequency > 1.0) {
3603            midPunctuationFrequency = 1.0 / midPunctuationFrequency;
3604        }
3605        if (maxChars < 4)
3606            return "!";
3607        if (maxChars <= 5 * minWords) {
3608            minWords = 1;
3609            maxWords = 1;
3610        }
3611        int frustration = 0;
3612        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(maxChars);
3613        String next = word(rng, true);
3614        while (next.length() >= maxChars - 1 && frustration < 50) {
3615            next = word(rng, true);
3616            frustration++;
3617        }
3618        if (frustration >= 50) return "!";
3619        sb.append(next);
3620        for (int i = 1; i < minWords && frustration < 50 && sb.length() < maxChars - 7; i++) {
3621            if (rng.nextDouble() < midPunctuationFrequency && sb.length() < maxChars - 3) {
3622                sb.append(rng.getRandomElement(midPunctuation));
3623            }
3624            next = word(rng, false);
3625            while (sb.length() + next.length() >= maxChars - 2 && frustration < 50) {
3626                next = word(rng, false);
3627                frustration++;
3628            }
3629            if (frustration >= 50) break;
3630            sb.append(' ').append(next);
3631        }
3632        for (int i = minWords; i < maxWords && sb.length() < maxChars - 7 && rng.nextInt(2 * maxWords) > i && frustration < 50; i++) {
3633            if (rng.nextDouble() < midPunctuationFrequency && sb.length() < maxChars - 3) {
3634                sb.append(rng.getRandomElement(midPunctuation));
3635            }
3636            next = word(rng, false);
3637            while (sb.length() + next.length() >= maxChars - 2 && frustration < 50) {
3638                next = word(rng, false);
3639                frustration++;
3640            }
3641            if (frustration >= 50) break;
3642            sb.append(' ');
3643            sb.append(next);
3644        }
3645
3646        if (endPunctuation != null && endPunctuation.length > 0) {
3647
3648            next = rng.getRandomElement(endPunctuation);
3649            if (sb.length() + next.length() >= maxChars)
3650                sb.append('.');
3651            else
3652                sb.append(next);
3653        }
3654
3655        if (sb.length() > maxChars)
3656            return "!";
3657        return sb.toString();
3658    }

3660    protected String[] merge1000(IRNG rng, String[] me, String[] other, double otherInfluence) {
3661        if (other.length <= 0 && me.length <= 0)
3662            return new String[]{};
3663        String[] ret = new String[1000];
3664        int otherCount = (int) (1000 * otherInfluence);
3665        int idx = 0;
3666        if (other.length > 0) {
3667            String[] tmp = new String[other.length];
3668            rng.shuffle(other, tmp);
3669            for (idx = 0; idx < otherCount; idx++) {
3670                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3671            }
3672        }
3673        if (me.length > 0) {
3674            String[] tmp = new String[me.length];
3675            rng.shuffle(me, tmp);
3676            for (; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3677                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3678            }
3679        } else {
3680            for (; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3681                ret[idx] = other[idx % other.length];
3682            }
3683        }
3684        return ret;
3685    }

3688    protected String[] accentVowels(IRNG rng, String[] me, double influence) {
3689        String[] ret = new String[1000];
3690        int otherCount = (int) (1000 * influence);
3691        int idx = 0;
3692        Matcher matcher;
3693        if (me.length > 0) {
3694            String[] tmp = new String[me.length];
3695            rng.shuffle(me, tmp);
3696            for (idx = 0; idx < otherCount; idx++) {
3697                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length]
3698                        .replace('a', accentedVowels[0][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[0].length)])
3699                        .replace('e', accentedVowels[1][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[1].length)])
3700                        .replace('i', accentedVowels[2][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[2].length)])
3701                        .replace('o', accentedVowels[3][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[3].length)])
3702                        .replace('u', accentedVowels[4][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[4].length)]);
3703                matcher = repeats.matcher(ret[idx]);
3704                if (matcher.find()) {
3705                    ret[idx] = matcher.replaceAll(rng.getRandomElement(me));
3706                }
3707            }
3708            for (; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3709                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3710            }
3711        } else
3712            return new String[]{};
3713        return ret;
3714    }
3715
3716    protected String[] accentConsonants(IRNG rng, String[] me, double influence) {
3717        String[] ret = new String[1000];
3718        int otherCount = (int) (1000 * influence);
3719        int idx = 0;
3720        Matcher matcher;
3721        if (me.length > 0) {
3722            String[] tmp = new String[me.length];
3723            rng.shuffle(me, tmp);
3724            for (idx = 0; idx < otherCount; idx++) {
3725                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length]
3726                        //0
3727                        .replace('c', accentedConsonants[1][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[1].length)])
3728                        .replace('d', accentedConsonants[2][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[2].length)])
3729                        .replace('f', accentedConsonants[3][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[3].length)])
3730                        .replace('g', accentedConsonants[4][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[4].length)])
3731                        .replace('h', accentedConsonants[5][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[5].length)])
3732                        .replace('j', accentedConsonants[6][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[6].length)])
3733                        .replace('k', accentedConsonants[7][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[7].length)])
3734                        .replace('l', accentedConsonants[8][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[8].length)])
3735                        //9
3736                        .replace('n', accentedConsonants[10][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[10].length)])
3737                        //11
3738                        //12
3739                        .replace('r', accentedConsonants[13][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[13].length)])
3740                        .replace('s', accentedConsonants[14][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[14].length)])
3741                        .replace('t', accentedConsonants[15][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[15].length)])
3742                        //16
3743                        .replace('w', accentedConsonants[17][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[17].length)])
3744                        //18
3745                        .replace('y', accentedConsonants[19][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[19].length)])
3746                        .replace('z', accentedConsonants[20][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[20].length)]);
3747
3748                matcher = repeats.matcher(ret[idx]);
3749                if (matcher.find()) {
3750                    ret[idx] = matcher.replaceAll(rng.getRandomElement(me));
3751                }
3752            }
3753            for (; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3754                ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3755            }
3756        } else
3757            return new String[]{};
3758        return ret;
3759    }
3760
3761    protected String[] accentBoth(IRNG rng, String[] me, double vowelInfluence, double consonantInfluence) {
3762        String[] ret = new String[1000];
3763        int idx = 0;
3764        Matcher matcher;
3765        if (me.length > 0) {
3766            String[] tmp = new String[me.length];
3767            rng.shuffle(me, tmp);
3768            for (idx = 0; idx < 1000; idx++) {
3769                boolean subVowel = rng.nextDouble() < vowelInfluence, subCon = rng.nextDouble() < consonantInfluence;
3770                if (subVowel && subCon) {
3771                    ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length]
3772                            .replace('a', accentedVowels[0][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[0].length)])
3773                            .replace('e', accentedVowels[1][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[1].length)])
3774                            .replace('i', accentedVowels[2][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[2].length)])
3775                            .replace('o', accentedVowels[3][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[3].length)])
3776                            .replace('u', accentedVowels[4][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[4].length)])
3777
3778                            //0
3779                            .replace('c', accentedConsonants[1][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[1].length)])
3780                            .replace('d', accentedConsonants[2][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[2].length)])
3781                            .replace('f', accentedConsonants[3][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[3].length)])
3782                            .replace('g', accentedConsonants[4][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[4].length)])
3783                            .replace('h', accentedConsonants[5][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[5].length)])
3784                            .replace('j', accentedConsonants[6][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[6].length)])
3785                            .replace('k', accentedConsonants[7][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[7].length)])
3786                            .replace('l', accentedConsonants[8][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[8].length)])
3787                            //9
3788                            .replace('n', accentedConsonants[10][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[10].length)])
3789                            //11
3790                            //12
3791                            .replace('r', accentedConsonants[13][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[13].length)])
3792                            .replace('s', accentedConsonants[14][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[14].length)])
3793                            .replace('t', accentedConsonants[15][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[15].length)])
3794                            //16
3795                            .replace('w', accentedConsonants[17][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[17].length)])
3796                            //18
3797                            .replace('y', accentedConsonants[19][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[19].length)])
3798                            .replace('z', accentedConsonants[20][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[20].length)]);
3799
3800                    matcher = repeats.matcher(ret[idx]);
3801                    if (matcher.find()) {
3802                        ret[idx] = matcher.replaceAll(rng.getRandomElement(me));
3803                    }
3804                } else if (subVowel) {
3805                    ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length]
3806                            .replace('a', accentedVowels[0][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[0].length)])
3807                            .replace('e', accentedVowels[1][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[1].length)])
3808                            .replace('i', accentedVowels[2][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[2].length)])
3809                            .replace('o', accentedVowels[3][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[3].length)])
3810                            .replace('u', accentedVowels[4][rng.nextInt(accentedVowels[4].length)]);
3811
3812                    matcher = repeats.matcher(ret[idx]);
3813                    if (matcher.find()) {
3814                        ret[idx] = matcher.replaceAll(rng.getRandomElement(me));
3815                    }
3816                } else if (subCon) {
3817                    ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length]
3818                            //0
3819                            .replace('c', accentedConsonants[1][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[1].length)])
3820                            .replace('d', accentedConsonants[2][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[2].length)])
3821                            .replace('f', accentedConsonants[3][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[3].length)])
3822                            .replace('g', accentedConsonants[4][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[4].length)])
3823                            .replace('h', accentedConsonants[5][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[5].length)])
3824                            .replace('j', accentedConsonants[6][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[6].length)])
3825                            .replace('k', accentedConsonants[7][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[7].length)])
3826                            .replace('l', accentedConsonants[8][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[8].length)])
3827                            //9
3828                            .replace('n', accentedConsonants[10][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[10].length)])
3829                            //11
3830                            //12
3831                            .replace('r', accentedConsonants[13][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[13].length)])
3832                            .replace('s', accentedConsonants[14][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[14].length)])
3833                            .replace('t', accentedConsonants[15][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[15].length)])
3834                            //16
3835                            .replace('w', accentedConsonants[17][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[17].length)])
3836                            //18
3837                            .replace('y', accentedConsonants[19][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[19].length)])
3838                            .replace('z', accentedConsonants[20][rng.nextInt(accentedConsonants[20].length)]);
3839
3840                    matcher = repeats.matcher(ret[idx]);
3841                    if (matcher.find()) {
3842                        ret[idx] = matcher.replaceAll(rng.getRandomElement(me));
3843                    }
3844                } else ret[idx] = tmp[idx % tmp.length];
3845
3846            }
3847        } else
3848            return new String[]{};
3849        return ret;
3850    }
3851
3852    /**
3853     * Makes a new FakeLanguageGen that mixes this object with {@code other}, mingling the consonants and vowels they
3854     * use as well as any word suffixes or other traits, and favoring the qualities in {@code other} by
3855     * {@code otherInfluence}, which will value both languages evenly if it is 0.5 . 
3856     * @param other another FakeLanguageGen to mix along with this one into a new language
3857     * @param otherInfluence how much other should affect the pair, with 0.5 being equal and 1.0 being only other used
3858     * @return a new FakeLanguageGen with traits from both languages
3859     */
3860    public FakeLanguageGen mix(FakeLanguageGen other, double otherInfluence) {
3861        otherInfluence = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(otherInfluence, 1.0));
3862        double myInfluence = 1.0 - otherInfluence;
3863
3864        RNG rng = new RNG((hash64() & 0xffffffffL) | ((other.hash64() & 0xffffffffL) << 32)
3865                ^ NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(otherInfluence));
3866
3867        String[] ov = merge1000(rng, openingVowels, other.openingVowels, otherInfluence),
3868                mv = merge1000(rng, midVowels, other.midVowels, otherInfluence),
3869                oc = merge1000(rng, openingConsonants, other.openingConsonants, otherInfluence *
3870                        Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, 1.0 - other.vowelStartFrequency + vowelStartFrequency))),
3871                mc = merge1000(rng, midConsonants, other.midConsonants, otherInfluence),
3872                cc = merge1000(rng, closingConsonants, other.closingConsonants, otherInfluence *
3873                        Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, 1.0 - other.vowelEndFrequency + vowelEndFrequency))),
3874                cs = merge1000(rng, closingSyllables, other.closingSyllables, otherInfluence *
3875                        Math.max(0.0, Math.min(1.0, other.syllableEndFrequency - syllableEndFrequency))),
3876                splitters = merge1000(rng, vowelSplitters, other.vowelSplitters, otherInfluence);
3877
3878        IntDoubleOrderedMap freqs = new IntDoubleOrderedMap(syllableFrequencies);
3879        for (IntDoubleOrderedMap.MapEntry kv : other.syllableFrequencies.mapEntrySet()) {
3880            if (freqs.containsKey(kv.getIntKey()))
3881                freqs.put(kv.getIntKey(), kv.getDoubleValue() + freqs.get(kv.getIntKey()));
3882            else
3883                freqs.put(kv.getIntKey(), kv.getDoubleValue());
3884        }
3885        List<Modifier> mods = new ArrayList<>(modifiers.size() + other.modifiers.size());
3886        mods.addAll(modifiers);
3887        mods.addAll(other.modifiers);
3888        return new FakeLanguageGen(ov, mv, oc, mc, cc, cs, splitters, freqs,
3889                vowelStartFrequency * myInfluence + other.vowelStartFrequency * otherInfluence,
3890                vowelEndFrequency * myInfluence + other.vowelEndFrequency * otherInfluence,
3891                vowelSplitFrequency * myInfluence + other.vowelSplitFrequency * otherInfluence,
3892                syllableEndFrequency * myInfluence + other.syllableEndFrequency * otherInfluence,
3893                (sanityChecks == null) ? other.sanityChecks : sanityChecks, true, mods)
3894                .setName(otherInfluence > 0.5 ? other.name + "/" + name : name + "/" + other.name);
3895    }
3896
3897    private static double readDouble(Object o) {
3898        if (o instanceof Double) return (Double) o;
3899        else if (o instanceof Float) return (Float) o;
3900        else if (o instanceof Long) return ((Long) o).doubleValue();
3901        else if (o instanceof Integer) return (Integer) o;
3902        else if (o instanceof Short) return (Short) o;
3903        else if (o instanceof Byte) return (Byte) o;
3904        else if (o instanceof Character) return (Character) o;
3905        return 0.0;
3906    }
3907
3908    /**
3909     * Produces a FakeLanguageGen by mixing this FakeLanguageGen with one or more other FakeLanguageGen objects. Takes
3910     * a weight for this, another FakeLanguageGen, a weight for that FakeLanguageGen, then a possibly-empty group of
3911     * FakeLanguageGen parameters and the weights for those parameters. If other1 is null or if pairs has been given a
3912     * value of null instead of the normal (possibly empty) array of Objects, then this simply returns a copy of this
3913     * FakeLanguageGen. Otherwise, it will at least mix this language with other1 using the given weights for each.
3914     * If pairs is not empty, it has special requirements for what types it allows and in what order, but does no type
3915     * checking. Specifically, pairs requires the first Object to be a FakeLanguageGen, the next to be a number of some
3916     * kind that will be the weight for the previous FakeLanguageGen(this method can handle non-Double weights, and
3917     * converts them to Double if needed), and every two parameters after that to follow the same order and pattern
3918     * (FakeLanguageGen, then number, then FakeLanguageGen, then number...). Weights are absolute, and don't depend on
3919     * earlier weights, which is the case when chaining the {@link #mix(FakeLanguageGen, double)} method. This makes
3920     * reasoning about the ideal weights for multiple mixed languages easier; to mix 3 languages equally you can use
3921     * 3 equal weights with this, whereas with mix chaining you would need to mix the first two with 0.5 and the third
3922     * with 0.33 .
3923     * <br>
3924     * Unlike the static method {@link #mixAll(Object...)}, this _is_ intended for external use, in part because the
3925     * technique for mixing languages by weight is so much more intuitive, but also because this assigns valid data for
3926     * serializing and deserializing this FakeLanguageGen that allows it to use significantly less space (less than 1/72
3927     * the bytes used in one not-quite-simple test).
3928     *
3929     * @param myWeight the weight to assign this FakeLanguageGen in the mix
3930     * @param other1   another FakeLanguageGen to mix in; if null, this method will abort and return {@link #copy()}
3931     * @param weight1  the weight to assign other1 in the mix
3932     * @param pairs    may be empty, not null; otherwise must alternate between FakeLanguageGen and number (weight) elements
3933     * @return a FakeLanguageGen produced by mixing this with any FakeLanguageGen arguments by the given weights
3934     */
3935    public FakeLanguageGen mix(double myWeight, FakeLanguageGen other1, double weight1, Object... pairs) {
3936        if (other1 == null || pairs == null)
3937            return copy();
3938        OrderedSet<Modifier> mods = new OrderedSet<>(modifiers);
3939        FakeLanguageGen mixer = removeModifiers();
3940        FakeLanguageGen[] languages = new FakeLanguageGen[2 + (pairs.length >>> 1)];
3941        double[] weights = new double[languages.length];
3942        String[] summaries = new String[languages.length];
3943        boolean summarize = true;
3944        double total = 0.0, current, weight;
3945        languages[0] = mixer;
3946        total += weights[0] = myWeight;
3947        if ((summaries[0] = mixer.summary) == null) summarize = false;
3948        mods.addAll(other1.modifiers);
3949        languages[1] = other1.removeModifiers();
3950        total += weights[1] = weight1;
3951        if (summarize && (summaries[1] = languages[1].summary) == null) summarize = false;
3952        for (int i = 1, p = 2; i < pairs.length; i += 2, p++) {
3953            if (pairs[i] == null || pairs[i - 1] == null)
3954                continue;
3955            languages[p] = ((FakeLanguageGen) pairs[i - 1]).removeModifiers();
3956            total += weights[p] = readDouble(pairs[i]);
3957            if (summarize && (summaries[p] = languages[p].summary) == null) summarize = false;
3958        }
3959        if (total == 0)
3960            return copy();
3961        current = myWeight / total;
3962        for (int i = 1; i < languages.length; i++) {
3963            if ((weight = weights[i]) > 0)
3964                mixer = mixer.mix(languages[i], weight / total / (current += weight / total));
3965        }
3966        if (summarize) {
3967            StringBuilder brief = new StringBuilder(64);
3968            String c;
3969            int idx;
3970            for (int i = 0; i < summaries.length; i++) {
3971                c = summaries[i];
3972                idx = c.indexOf('@');
3973                if (idx >= 0) {
3974                    brief.append(c, 0, idx + 1).append(weights[i]);
3975                    if (i < summaries.length - 1)
3976                        brief.append('~');
3977                }
3978            }
3979            for (int i = 0; i < mods.size(); i++) {
3980                brief.append('℗').append(mods.getAt(i).serializeToString());
3981            }
3982            return mixer.addModifiers(mods).summarize(brief.toString());
3983        } else
3984            return mixer.addModifiers(mods);
3985    }
3986
3987    /**
3988     * Produces a FakeLanguageGen from a group of FakeLanguageGen parameters and the weights for those parameters.
3989     * Requires the first Object in pairs to be a FakeLanguageGen, the next to be a number of some kind that will be the
3990     * weight for the previous FakeLanguageGen(this method can handle non-Double weights, and converts them to Double
3991     * if needed), and every two parameters after that to follow the same order and pattern (FakeLanguageGen, then
3992     * number, then FakeLanguageGen, then number...). There should be at least 4 elements in pairs, half of them
3993     * languages and half of them weights, for this to do any mixing, but it can produce a result with as little as one
3994     * FakeLanguageGen (returning a copy of the first FakeLanguageGen). Weights are absolute, and don't depend on
3995     * earlier weights, which is the case when chaining the {@link #mix(FakeLanguageGen, double)} method. This makes
3996     * reasoning about the ideal weights for multiple mixed languages easier; to mix 3 languages equally you can use
3997     * 3 equal weights with this, whereas with mix chaining you would need to mix the first two with 0.5 and the third
3998     * with 0.33 .
3999     * <br>
4000     * Not intended for external use, but it could be useful. Used internally in the deserialization code.
4001     *
4002     * @param pairs should have at least one item, and must alternate between FakeLanguageGen and number (weight) elements
4003     * @return a FakeLanguageGen produced by mixing any FakeLanguageGen arguments by the given weights
4004     */
4005    public static FakeLanguageGen mixAll(Object... pairs) {
4006        int len;
4007        if (pairs == null || (len = pairs.length) <= 0)
4008            return ENGLISH.copy();
4009        if (len < 4)
4010            return ((FakeLanguageGen) pairs[0]).copy();
4011        Object[] pairs2 = new Object[len - 4];
4012        if (len > 4)
4013            System.arraycopy(pairs, 4, pairs2, 0, len - 4);
4014        return ((FakeLanguageGen) pairs[0]).mix(readDouble(pairs[1]), (FakeLanguageGen) pairs[2], readDouble(pairs[3]), pairs2);
4015    }
4016
4017    /**
4018     * Produces a new FakeLanguageGen like this one but with extra vowels and/or consonants possible, adding from a wide
4019     * selection of accented vowels (if vowelInfluence is above 0.0) and/or consonants (if consonantInfluence is above
4020     * 0.0). This may produce a gibberish-looking language with no rhyme or reason to the accents, and generally
4021     * consonantInfluence should be very low if it is above 0 at all.
4022     * @param vowelInfluence between 0.0 and 1.0; if 0.0 will not affect vowels at all
4023     * @param consonantInfluence between 0.0 and 1.0; if 0.0 will not affect consonants at all
4024     * @return a new FakeLanguageGen with modifications to add accented vowels and/or consonants
4025     */
4026    public FakeLanguageGen addAccents(double vowelInfluence, double consonantInfluence) {
4027        vowelInfluence = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(vowelInfluence, 1.0));
4028        consonantInfluence = Math.max(0.0, Math.min(consonantInfluence, 1.0));
4029
4030        RNG rng = new RNG((hash64() & 0xffffffffL) ^
4031                ((NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelInfluence) & 0xffffffffL) | (NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(consonantInfluence) << 32)));
4032        String[] ov = accentVowels(rng, openingVowels, vowelInfluence),
4033                mv = accentVowels(rng, midVowels, vowelInfluence),
4034                oc = accentConsonants(rng, openingConsonants, consonantInfluence),
4035                mc = accentConsonants(rng, midConsonants, consonantInfluence),
4036                cc = accentConsonants(rng, closingConsonants, consonantInfluence),
4037                cs = accentBoth(rng, closingSyllables, vowelInfluence, consonantInfluence);
4038
4039
4040        return new FakeLanguageGen(ov, mv, oc, mc, cc, cs, vowelSplitters, syllableFrequencies,
4041                vowelStartFrequency,
4042                vowelEndFrequency,
4043                vowelSplitFrequency,
4044                syllableEndFrequency, sanityChecks, clean, modifiers).setName(name + "-Bònüs");
4045    }
4046
4047    private static String[] copyStrings(String[] start) {
4048        String[] next = new String[start.length];
4049        System.arraycopy(start, 0, next, 0, start.length);
4050        return next;
4051    }
4052
4053    /**
4054     * Useful for cases with limited fonts, this produces a new FakeLanguageGen like this one but with all accented
4055     * characters removed (including almost all non-ASCII Latin-alphabet characters, but only some Greek and Cyrillic
4056     * characters). This will replace letters like "A with a ring" with just "A". Some of the letters chosen as
4057     * replacements aren't exact matches.
4058     * @return a new FakeLanguageGen like this one but without accented letters
4059     */
4060    public FakeLanguageGen removeAccents() {
4061
4062        String[] ov = copyStrings(openingVowels),
4063                mv = copyStrings(midVowels),
4064                oc = copyStrings(openingConsonants),
4065                mc = copyStrings(midConsonants),
4066                cc = copyStrings(closingConsonants),
4067                cs = copyStrings(closingSyllables);
4068        for (int i = 0; i < ov.length; i++) {
4069            ov[i] = removeAccents(openingVowels[i]).toString();
4070        }
4071        for (int i = 0; i < mv.length; i++) {
4072            mv[i] = removeAccents(midVowels[i]).toString();
4073        }
4074        for (int i = 0; i < oc.length; i++) {
4075            oc[i] = removeAccents(openingConsonants[i]).toString();
4076        }
4077        for (int i = 0; i < mc.length; i++) {
4078            mc[i] = removeAccents(midConsonants[i]).toString();
4079        }
4080        for (int i = 0; i < cc.length; i++) {
4081            cc[i] = removeAccents(closingConsonants[i]).toString();
4082        }
4083        for (int i = 0; i < cs.length; i++) {
4084            cs[i] = removeAccents(closingSyllables[i]).toString();
4085        }
4086
4087        return new FakeLanguageGen(ov, mv, oc, mc, cc, cs, vowelSplitters, syllableFrequencies,
4088                vowelStartFrequency,
4089                vowelEndFrequency,
4090                vowelSplitFrequency,
4091                syllableEndFrequency, sanityChecks, clean, modifiers);
4092    }

4094    /**
4095     * Returns the name of this FakeLanguageGen, such as "English" or "Deep Speech", if one was registered for this.
4096     * In the case of hybrid languages produced by {@link #mix(FakeLanguageGen, double)} or related methods, this should
4097     * produce a String like "English/French" (or "English/French/Maori" if more are mixed together). If no name was
4098     * registered, this will return "Nameless Language".
4099     * @return the human-readable name of this language, or "Nameless Language" if none is known
4100     */
4101    public String getName() {
4102        return name;
4103    }
4104    private FakeLanguageGen setName(final String languageName)
4105    {
4106        name = languageName;
4107        return this;
4108    }

4110    /**
4111     * Adds the specified Modifier objects from a Collection to a copy of this FakeLanguageGen and returns it.
4112     * You can obtain a Modifier with the static constants in the FakeLanguageGen.Modifier nested class, the
4113     * FakeLanguageGen.modifier() method, or Modifier's constructor.
4114     *
4115     * @param mods an array or vararg of Modifier objects
4116     * @return a copy of this with the Modifiers added
4117     */
4118    public FakeLanguageGen addModifiers(Collection<Modifier> mods) {
4119        FakeLanguageGen next = copy();
4120        next.modifiers.addAll(mods);
4121        return next;
4122    }
4123
4124    /**
4125     * Adds the specified Modifier objects to a copy of this FakeLanguageGen and returns it.
4126     * You can obtain a Modifier with the static constants in the FakeLanguageGen.Modifier nested class, the
4127     * FakeLanguageGen.modifier() method, or Modifier's constructor.
4128     *
4129     * @param mods an array or vararg of Modifier objects
4130     * @return a copy of this with the Modifiers added
4131     */
4132    public FakeLanguageGen addModifiers(Modifier... mods) {
4133        FakeLanguageGen next = copy();
4134        Collections.addAll(next.modifiers, mods);
4135        return next;
4136    }

4139     * Creates a copy of this FakeLanguageGen with no modifiers.
4140     *
4141     * @return a copy of this FakeLanguageGen with modifiers removed.
4142     */
4143    public FakeLanguageGen removeModifiers() {
4144        FakeLanguageGen next = copy();
4145        next.modifiers.clear();
4146        return next;
4147    }

4155    public static Modifier modifier(String pattern, String replacement) {

4162     * @param chance the chance, as a double between 0 and 1, that the Modifier will take effect
4163     * @return a Modifier that can be applied to a FakeLanguagGen

4165    public static Modifier modifier(String pattern, String replacement, double chance) {

4169    @Override
4170    public boolean equals(Object o) {
4171        if (this == o) return true;
4172        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
4173
4174        FakeLanguageGen that = (FakeLanguageGen) o;
4175
4176        if (clean != that.clean) return false;
4177        if (Double.compare(that.totalSyllableFrequency, totalSyllableFrequency) != 0) return false;
4178        if (Double.compare(that.vowelStartFrequency, vowelStartFrequency) != 0) return false;
4179        if (Double.compare(that.vowelEndFrequency, vowelEndFrequency) != 0) return false;
4180        if (Double.compare(that.vowelSplitFrequency, vowelSplitFrequency) != 0) return false;
4181        if (Double.compare(that.syllableEndFrequency, syllableEndFrequency) != 0) return false;
4182        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4183        if (!Arrays.equals(openingVowels, that.openingVowels)) return false;
4184        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4185        if (!Arrays.equals(midVowels, that.midVowels)) return false;
4186        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4187        if (!Arrays.equals(openingConsonants, that.openingConsonants)) return false;
4188        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4189        if (!Arrays.equals(midConsonants, that.midConsonants)) return false;
4190        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4191        if (!Arrays.equals(closingConsonants, that.closingConsonants)) return false;
4192        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4193        if (!Arrays.equals(vowelSplitters, that.vowelSplitters)) return false;
4194        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4195        if (!Arrays.equals(closingSyllables, that.closingSyllables)) return false;
4196        if (!syllableFrequencies.equals(that.syllableFrequencies)) return false;
4197        // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4198        if (!Arrays.equals(sanityChecks, that.sanityChecks)) return false;
4199        return modifiers != null ? modifiers.equals(that.modifiers) : that.modifiers == null;
4200    }
4201
4202    @Override
4203    public int hashCode() {
4204        int result;
4205        result = CrossHash.hash(openingVowels);
4206        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(midVowels);
4207        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(openingConsonants);
4208        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(midConsonants);
4209        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(closingConsonants);
4210        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(vowelSplitters);
4211        result = 31 * result + CrossHash.hash(closingSyllables);
4212        result = 31 * result + (clean ? 1 : 0);
4213        result = 31 * result + syllableFrequencies.hashCode();
4214        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(totalSyllableFrequency);
4215        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(vowelStartFrequency);
4216        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(vowelEndFrequency);
4217        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(vowelSplitFrequency);
4218        result = 31 * result + NumberTools.doubleToMixedIntBits(syllableEndFrequency);
4219        result = 31 * result + (sanityChecks != null ? sanityChecks.length + 1 : 0);
4220        result *= 31;
4221        if(modifiers != null) {
4222            for (int i = 0; i < modifiers.size(); i++) {
4223                result += 7 * (i + 1) * modifiers.get(i).hashCode();
4224            }
4225        }
4226        return result;
4227    }
4228    public long hash64() {
4229        long result           = CrossHash.hash64(openingVowels);
4230        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(midVowels);
4231        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(openingConsonants);
4232        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(midConsonants);
4233        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(closingConsonants);
4234        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(vowelSplitters);
4235        result = 31L * result + CrossHash.hash64(closingSyllables);
4236        result = 31L * result + (clean ? 1L : 0L);
4237        result = 31L * result + syllableFrequencies.hash64();
4238        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(totalSyllableFrequency);
4239        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelStartFrequency);
4240        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelEndFrequency);
4241        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(vowelSplitFrequency);
4242        result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(syllableEndFrequency);
4243        result = 31L * result + (sanityChecks != null ? sanityChecks.length + 1L : 0L);
4244        result *= 31L;
4245        if(modifiers != null) {
4246            for (int i = 0; i < modifiers.size(); i++) {
4247                result += 7L * (i + 1L) * CrossHash.hash64(modifiers.get(i).alterations);
4248            }
4249        }
4250        return result;
4251    }

4286
4287    public static FakeLanguageGen deserializeFromString(String data) {
4288        if (data == null || data.equals(""))
4289            return ENGLISH.copy();
4290        int poundIndex = data.indexOf('#'), snailIndex = data.indexOf('@'), tempBreak = data.indexOf('℗'),
4291                breakIndex = (tempBreak < 0) ? data.length() : tempBreak,
4292                tildeIndex = Math.min(data.indexOf('~'), breakIndex), prevTildeIndex = -1;
4293        if (tildeIndex < 0)
4294            tildeIndex = data.length();
4295
4296        if (snailIndex < 0)
4297            return ENGLISH.copy();
4298        ArrayList<Object> pairs = new ArrayList<>(4);
4299        while (snailIndex >= 0) {
4300            if (poundIndex >= 0 && poundIndex < snailIndex) // random case
4301            {
4302                pairs.add(randomLanguage(Long.parseLong(data.substring(poundIndex + 1, snailIndex))));
4303                pairs.add(Double.valueOf(data.substring(snailIndex + 1, tildeIndex)));
4304                poundIndex = -1;
4305            } else {
4306                pairs.add(registry.getAt(Integer.parseInt(data.substring(prevTildeIndex + 1, snailIndex))));
4307                pairs.add(Double.valueOf(data.substring(snailIndex + 1, tildeIndex)));
4308            }
4309            snailIndex = data.indexOf('@', snailIndex + 1);
4310            if (snailIndex > breakIndex)
4311                break;
4312            prevTildeIndex = tildeIndex;
4313            tildeIndex = Math.min(data.indexOf('~', tildeIndex + 1), breakIndex);
4314            if (tildeIndex < 0)
4315                tildeIndex = data.length();
4316        }
4317        ArrayList<Modifier> mods = new ArrayList<>(8);
4318        if (breakIndex == tempBreak) {
4319            tildeIndex = breakIndex - 1;
4320            while ((prevTildeIndex = data.indexOf('℗', tildeIndex + 1)) >= 0) {
4321                tildeIndex = data.indexOf('℗', prevTildeIndex + 1);
4322                if (tildeIndex < 0) tildeIndex = data.length();
4323                mods.add(Modifier.deserializeFromString(data.substring(prevTildeIndex, tildeIndex)));
4324            }
4325        }
4326        FakeLanguageGen flg = mixAll(pairs.toArray());
4327        flg.modifiers.addAll(mods);
4328        return flg;
4329    }
4330
4331    public static class Modifier implements Serializable {
4332        private static final long serialVersionUID = 1734863678490422371L;
4333        public final Alteration[] alterations;
4334
4335        public Modifier() {
4336            alterations = new Alteration[0];
4337        }
4338
4339        public Modifier(String pattern, String replacement) {
4340            alterations = new Alteration[]{new Alteration(pattern, replacement)};
4341        }
4342
4343        public Modifier(String pattern, String replacement, double chance) {
4344            alterations = new Alteration[]{new Alteration(pattern, replacement, chance)};
4345        }
4346
4347        public Modifier(Alteration... alts) {
4348            alterations = (alts == null) ? new Alteration[0] : alts;
4349        }
4350
4351        public StringBuilder modify(IRNG rng, StringBuilder sb) {
4352            Matcher m;
4353            Replacer.StringBuilderBuffer tb, working = Replacer.wrap(sb);
4354            StringBuilder tmp;
4355            boolean found;
4356            Alteration alt;
4357            for (int a = 0; a < alterations.length; a++) {
4358                alt = alterations[a];
4359                tmp = working.sb;
4360                tb = Replacer.wrap(new StringBuilder(tmp.length()));
4361                m = alt.replacer.getPattern().matcher(tmp);
4362
4363                found = false;
4364                while (true) {
4365                    if (alt.chance >= 1 || rng.nextDouble() < alt.chance) {
4366                        if (!Replacer.replaceStep(m, alt.replacer.getSubstitution(), tb))
4367                            break;
4368                        found = true;
4369                    } else {
4370                        if (!m.find())
4371                            break;
4372                        found = true;
4373                        m.getGroup(MatchResult.PREFIX, tb);
4374                        m.getGroup(MatchResult.MATCH, tb);
4375                        m.setTarget(m, MatchResult.SUFFIX);
4376                    }
4377                }
4378                if (found) {
4379                    m.getGroup(MatchResult.TARGET, tb);
4380                    working = tb;
4381                }
4382            }
4383            return working.sb;
4384        }

4425        /**
4426         * Removes accented letters and the two non-English consonants from text generated with {@link #NORSE}.
4427         * Replaces á, é, í, ý, ó, æ, ú, and ö with a, e, i, y, o, ae, and ou. In some instances, replaces j
4428         * with y. Replaces ð and þ with th and th, except for when preceded by s (then it replaces sð or sþ
4429         * with st or st) or when the start of a word is fð or fþ, where it replaces with fr or fr.
4430         */
4431        public static final Modifier SIMPLIFY_NORSE = replacementTable(
4432                "á", "a",
4433                "é", "e",
4434                "í", "i",
4435                "ý", "y",
4436                "ó", "o",
4437                "ú", "u",
4438                "æ", "ae",
4439                "ö", "ou",
4440                "([^aeiou])jy", "$1yai",
4441                "([^aeiou])j(?:[aeiouy]+)", "$1yo",
4442                "s([ðþ])", "st",
4443                "\\bf[ðþ]", "fr",
4444                "[ðþ]", "th");

4446        /**
4447         * Simple changes to merge "ae" into "æ", "oe" into "œ", and any of "aé", "áe", or "áé" into "ǽ".
4448         */
4449        public static final Modifier LIGATURES = replacementTable("ae", "æ", "oe", "œ", "[aá][eé]", "ǽ");
4450        /**
4451         * Some changes that can be applied when sanity checks (which force re-generating a new word) aren't appropriate
4452         * for fixing a word that isn't pronounceable.
4453         */
4454        public static final Modifier GENERAL_CLEANUP = replacementTable(
4455                "[æǽœìíîïĩīĭįıiùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy]([æǽœýÿŷỳy])", "$1",
4456                "q([ùúûüũūŭůűųu])$", "q$1e",
4457                "([ìíîïĩīĭįıi])[ìíîïĩīĭįıi]", "$1",
4458                "([æǽœìíîïĩīĭįıiùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy])[wŵẁẃẅ]$", "$1",
4459                "([ùúûüũūŭůűųu])([òóôõöøōŏőǿo])", "$2$1",
4460                "[àáâãäåāăąǻaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy]([æǽœ])", "$1",
4461                "([æǽœ])[àáâãäåāăąǻaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy]", "$1",
4462                "([wŵẁẃẅ])[wŵẁẃẅ]", "$1",
4463                "qq", "q");

4465        //àáâãäåāăąǻæǽaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőœǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳy
4466        //bcçćĉċčdþðďđḍfgĝğġģhĥħḥjĵȷkķlĺļľŀłḷḹmṃnñńņňŋṅṇpqrŕŗřṛṝsśŝşšșṣtţťțṭvwŵẁẃẅxyýÿŷỳzźżž

4468        /**
4469         * Creates a Modifier that will replace the nth char in initial with the nth char in change. Expects initial and
4470         * change to be the same length, but will use the lesser length if they are not equal-length. Because of the
4471         * state of the text at the time modifiers are run, only lower-case letters need to be searched for.
4472         *
4473         * @param initial a String containing lower-case letters or other symbols to be swapped out of a text
4474         * @param change  a String containing characters that will replace occurrences of characters in initial
4475         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4476         */
4477        public static Modifier charReplacementTable(String initial, String change) {
4478            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[Math.min(initial.length(), change.length())];
4479            for (int i = 0; i < alts.length; i++) {
4480                //literal string syntax; avoids sensitive escaping issues and also doesn't need a character class,
4481                // which is slightly slower and has some odd escaping cases.
4482                alts[i] = new Alteration("\\Q" + initial.charAt(i), change.substring(i, i + 1));
4483            }
4484            return new Modifier(alts);
4485        }
4486
4487        /**
4488         * Creates a Modifier that will replace the nth String key in map with the nth value. Because of the
4489         * state of the text at the time modifiers are run, only lower-case letters need to be searched for.
4490         * This overload of replacementTable allows full regex pattern strings as keys and replacement syntax,
4491         * such as searching for "([aeiou])\\1+" to find repeated occurrences of the same vowel, and "$1" in
4492         * this example to replace the repeated section with only the first vowel.
4493         * The ordering of map matters if a later key contains an earlier key (the earlier one will be replaced
4494         * first, possibly making the later key not match), or if an earlier replacement causes a later one to
4495         * become valid.
4496         *
4497         * @param map containing String keys to replace and String values to use instead; replacements happen in order
4498         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4499         */
4500        public static Modifier replacementTable(OrderedMap<String, String> map) {
4501            if (map == null)
4502                return new Modifier();
4503            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[map.size()];
4504            for (int i = 0; i < alts.length; i++) {
4505                alts[i] = new Alteration(map.keyAt(i), map.getAt(i));
4506            }
4507            return new Modifier(alts);
4508        }
4509
4510        /**
4511         * Creates a Modifier that will replace the (n*2)th String in pairs with the (n*2+1)th value in pairs. Because
4512         * of the state of the text at the time modifiers are run, only lower-case letters need to be searched for.
4513         * This overload of replacementTable allows full regex syntax for search and replacement Strings,
4514         * such as searching for "([aeiou])\\1+" to find repeated occurrences of the same vowel, and "$1" in
4515         * this example to replace the repeated section with only the first vowel.
4516         * The ordering of pairs matters if a later search contains an earlier search (the earlier one will be replaced
4517         * first, possibly making the later search not match), or if an earlier replacement causes a later one to
4518         * become valid.
4519         *
4520         * @param pairs array or vararg of alternating Strings to search for and Strings to replace with; replacements happen in order
4521         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4522         */
4523        public static Modifier replacementTable(String... pairs) {
4524            int len;
4525            if (pairs == null || (len = pairs.length) <= 1)
4526                return new Modifier();
4527            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[len >> 1];
4528            for (int i = 0; i < alts.length; i++) {
4529                alts[i] = new Alteration(pairs[i<< 1], pairs[i<<1|1]);
4530            }
4531            return new Modifier(alts);
4532        }
4533
4534        /**
4535         * Adds the potential for the String {@code insertion} to be used as a vowel in addition to the vowels that the
4536         * language already uses; insertion will replace an existing vowel (at any point in a word that had a vowel
4537         * generated) with a probability of {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.1 at most) unless you want the
4538         * newly-inserted vowel to be likely to be present in every word of some sentences.
4539         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional vowel
4540         * @param chance the chance for a vowel cluster to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.1 or less
4541         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4542         */
4543        public static Modifier insertVowel(String insertion, double chance)
4544        {
4545            return new Modifier(anyVowelCluster, insertion, chance);
4546        }
4547
4548        /**
4549         * Adds the potential for the String {@code insertion} to be used as a consonant in addition to the consonants
4550         * that the language already uses; insertion will replace an existing consonant (at any point in a word that had
4551         * a consonant generated) with a probability of {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.1 at most) unless you
4552         * want the newly-inserted consonant to be likely to be present in every word of some sentences.
4553         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional consonant
4554         * @param chance the chance for a consonant cluster to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.1 or less
4555         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4556         */
4557        public static Modifier insertConsonant(String insertion, double chance)
4558        {
4559            return new Modifier(anyConsonantCluster, insertion, chance);
4560        }
4561
4562        /**
4563         * Adds the potential for the String {@code insertion} to be used as a vowel in addition to the vowels that the
4564         * language already uses; insertion will replace an existing vowel at the start of a word with a probability of
4565         * {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.2 at most) unless you want the newly-inserted vowel to be likely
4566         * to start every word of some sentences. Not all languages can start words with vowels, or do that very rarely,
4567         * so this might not do anything.
4568         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional opening vowel
4569         * @param chance the chance for a vowel cluster at the start of a word to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.2 or less
4570         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4571         */
4572        public static Modifier insertOpeningVowel(String insertion, double chance)
4573        {
4574            return new Modifier("\\b[àáâãäåæāăąǻǽaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőœǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳyαοειυаеёийоуъыэюя]+", insertion, chance);
4575        }
4576
4577        /**
4578         * Adds the potential for the String {@code insertion} to be used as a consonant in addition to the consonants
4579         * that the language already uses; insertion will replace an existing consonant at the start of a word with a
4580         * probability of {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.2 at most) unless you want the newly-inserted
4581         * consonant to be likely to start every word of some sentences. Not all languages can start words with
4582         * consonants, or do that very rarely, so this might not do anything.
4583         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional opening consonant
4584         * @param chance the chance for a consonant cluster at the start of a word to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.2 or less
4585         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4586         */
4587        public static Modifier insertOpeningConsonant(String insertion, double chance)
4588        {
4589            return new Modifier("\\b[bcçćĉċčdþðďđfgĝğġģhĥħjĵȷkķlĺļľŀłmnñńņňŋpqrŕŗřsśŝşšștţťțvwŵẁẃẅxyýÿŷỳzźżžṛṝḷḹḍṭṅṇṣṃḥρσζτκχνθμπψβλγφξςбвгдклпрстфхцжмнзчшщ]+", insertion, chance);
4590        }
4591
4592        /**
4593         * Adds the potential for the String {@code insertion} to be used as a vowel in addition to the vowels that the
4594         * language already uses; insertion will replace an existing vowel at the end of a word with a probability of
4595         * {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.2 at most) unless you want the newly-inserted vowel to be likely
4596         * to end every word of some sentences. Not all languages can end words with vowels, or do that very
4597         * rarely, so this might not do anything.
4598         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional closing vowel
4599         * @param chance the chance for a vowel cluster at the end of a word to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.2 or less
4600         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4601         */
4602        public static Modifier insertClosingVowel(String insertion, double chance)
4603        {
4604            return new Modifier("[àáâãäåæāăąǻǽaèéêëēĕėęěeìíîïĩīĭįıiòóôõöøōŏőœǿoùúûüũūŭůűųuýÿŷỳyαοειυаеёийоуъыэюя]+\\b", insertion, chance);
4605        }
4606
4607        /**
4608         * Adds the potential for the String {@code insertion} to be used as a consonant in addition to the consonants
4609         * that the language already uses; insertion will replace an existing consonant at the end of a word with a
4610         * probability of {@code chance}, so chance should be low (0.2 at most) unless you want the newly-inserted
4611         * consonant to be likely to end every word of some sentences. Not all languages can end words with consonants,
4612         * or do that very rarely, so this might not do anything.
4613         * @param insertion the String to use as an additional closing consonant
4614         * @param chance the chance for a consonant cluster at the end of a word to be replaced with insertion; normally 0.2 or less
4615         * @return a Modifier that can be added to a FakeLanguageGen with its addModifiers() method
4616         */
4617        public static Modifier insertClosingConsonant(String insertion, double chance)
4618        {
4619            return new Modifier("[bcçćĉċčdþðďđfgĝğġģhĥħjĵȷkķlĺļľŀłmnñńņňŋpqrŕŗřsśŝşšștţťțvwŵẁẃẅxyýÿŷỳzźżžṛṝḷḹḍṭṅṇṣṃḥρσζτκχνθμπψβλγφξςбвгдклпрстфхцжмнзчшщ]+\\b", insertion, chance);
4620        }
4621
4622        /**
4623         * This was used in an earlier version, which attempted to use a Romanization technique that would use Greek
4624         * letters and several accented Latin letters to try to accurately represent some of the complex orthography of
4625         * Arabic, but because FakeLanguageGen doesn't use that technique any more (it was effectively unreadable), this
4626         * Modifier is a no-op. Its use is never needed any more.
4627         * @deprecated This Modifier doesn't do anything, and isn't needed.
4628         */
4629        @Deprecated
4630        public static final Modifier SIMPLIFY_ARABIC = new Modifier(
4631                /*
4632                new Alteration("ţ", "th"),
4633                new Alteration("ĥ", "kh"),
4634                new Alteration("ħ", "khr"),
4635                new Alteration("đ", "dh"),
4636                new Alteration("ď", "dt"),
4637                new Alteration("š", "sh"),
4638                new Alteration("ş", "shw"),
4639                new Alteration("ť", "ch"),
4640                new Alteration("ż", "zh"),
4641                new Alteration("ξ", "khm"),
4642                new Alteration("δ", "gh"),
4643                new Alteration("ā", "aa"),
4644                new Alteration("ū", "uu"),
4645                new Alteration("ī", "ii")*/);
4646
4647        @Override
4648        public boolean equals(Object o) {
4649            if (this == o) return true;
4650            if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
4651
4652            Modifier modifier = (Modifier) o;
4653
4654            // Probably incorrect - comparing Object[] arrays with Arrays.equals
4655            return Arrays.equals(alterations, modifier.alterations);
4656        }
4657
4658        @Override
4659        public int hashCode() {
4660            return CrossHash.hash(alterations);
4661        }
4662
4663        @Override
4664        public String toString() {
4665            return "Modifier{" +
4666                    "alterations=" + Arrays.toString(alterations) +
4667                    '}';
4668        }
4669
4670        public String serializeToString() {
4671            if (alterations == null || alterations.length == 0) return "\6";
4672            StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder(32).append('\6');
4673            for (int i = 0; i < alterations.length; i++)
4674                sb.append(alterations[i].serializeToString()).append('\6');
4675            return sb.toString();
4676        }
4677
4678        public static Modifier deserializeFromString(String data) {
4679            int currIdx = data.indexOf(6), altIdx = currIdx, matches = 0;
4680            while (currIdx >= 0) {
4681                if ((currIdx = data.indexOf(6, currIdx + 1)) < 0)
4682                    break;
4683                matches++;
4684            }
4685            Alteration[] alts = new Alteration[matches];
4686            for (int i = 0; i < matches; i++) {
4687                alts[i] = Alteration.deserializeFromString(data.substring(altIdx + 1, altIdx = data.indexOf(6, altIdx + 1)));
4688            }
4689            return new Modifier(alts);
4690        }
4691    }
4692
4693    public static class Alteration implements Serializable {
4694        private static final long serialVersionUID = -2138854697837563188L;
4695        public Replacer replacer;
4696        public String replacement;
4697        public double chance;
4698
4699        public Alteration() {
4700            this("[tţťțṭ]?[sśŝşšș]+h?", "th");
4701        }
4702
4703        public Alteration(String pattern, String replacement) {
4704            this.replacement = replacement;
4705            replacer = Pattern.compile(pattern).replacer(replacement);
4706            chance = 1.0;
4707        }
4708
4709        public Alteration(String pattern, String replacement, double chance) {
4710            this.replacement = replacement;
4711            replacer = Pattern.compile(pattern).replacer(replacement);
4712            this.chance = chance;
4713        }
4714
4715        public Alteration(Pattern pattern, String replacement, double chance) {
4716            this.replacement = replacement;
4717            replacer = pattern.replacer(replacement);
4718            this.chance = chance;
4719        }
4720
4721        @Override
4722        public boolean equals(Object o) {
4723            if (this == o) return true;
4724            if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) return false;
4725
4726            Alteration that = (Alteration) o;
4727
4728            if (Double.compare(that.chance, chance) != 0) return false;
4729            return replacer.equals(that.replacer);
4730
4731        }
4732
4733        @Override
4734        public int hashCode() {
4735            long result;
4736            result = CrossHash.hash64(replacer.getPattern().serializeToString());
4737            result = 31L * result + NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(chance);
4738            result ^= result >>> 32;
4739            return (int) (0xFFFFFFFFL & result);
4740        }
4741
4742        @Override
4743        public String toString() {
4744            return "Alteration{" +
4745                    "replacer=" + replacer +
4746                    ", chance=" + chance +
4747                    '}';
4748        }
4749
4750        public String serializeToString() {
4751            return replacer.getPattern().serializeToString() + '\2' + replacement + '\4' + chance;
4752        }
4753
4754        public static Alteration deserializeFromString(String data) {
4755            int split2 = data.indexOf('\2'), split4 = data.indexOf('\4');
4756            return new Alteration(Pattern.deserializeFromString(data.substring(0, split2)),
4757                    data.substring(split2 + 1, split4),
4758                    Double.parseDouble(data.substring(split4 + 1)));
4759        }
4760    }
4761
4762    /**
4763     * A simple way to bundle a FakeLanguageGen with the arguments that would be passed to it when calling
4764     * {@link FakeLanguageGen#sentence(IRNG, int, int, String[], String[], double, int)} or one of its overloads.
4765     * You can call {@link #sentence()} on this to produce another String sentence with the parameters it was given
4766     * at construction. The parameters to
4767     * {@link #SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen, StatefulRNG, int, int, String[], String[], double, int)} are stored in fields of
4768     * the same name, and all fields in this class are public and modifiable.
4769     */
4770    public static class SentenceForm implements Serializable
4771    {
4772        private static final long serialVersionUID = 1246527948419533147L;
4773        public StatefulRNG rng;
4774        public int minWords, maxWords, maxChars;
4775        public String[] midPunctuation, endPunctuation;
4776        public double midPunctuationFrequency;
4777        public FakeLanguageGen language;
4778
4779        /**
4780         * Builds a SentenceForm with all default fields, using {@link FakeLanguageGen#FANTASY_NAME} for a language,
4781         * using between 1 and 9 words in a sentence, and otherwise defaulting to how
4782         * {@link #SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen, int, int)} behaves.
4783         */
4784        public SentenceForm()
4785        {
4786            this(FakeLanguageGen.FANTASY_NAME, FakeLanguageGen.srng, 1, 9,
4787                    mid,
4788                    end, 0.18, -1);
4789        }
4790        /**
4791         * Builds a SentenceForm with only a few fields specified. The {@link #rng} will be made based on
4792         * FakeLanguageGen's static {@link FakeLanguageGen#srng} field, maxChars will be -1 so the sentence length
4793         * will be limited only by maxWords and the length of words produced, and the between-word and end-of-sentence
4794         * punctuation will be set to reasonable defaults. This places either a comma or a semicolon after a word in the
4795         * middle of a sentence about 18% of the time ({@code midPunctuationFrequency} is 0.18), and can end a sentence
4796         * in a period, exclamation mark, question mark, or ellipsis (the "..." punctuation).
4797         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4798         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4799         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4800         */
4801        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, int minWords, int maxWords)
4802        {
4803            this(language, FakeLanguageGen.srng, minWords, maxWords, mid,
4804                    end, 0.18, -1);
4805        }
4806        /**
4807         * Builds a SentenceForm with all fields specified except for {@link #rng}, which will be made based on
4808         * FakeLanguageGen's static {@link FakeLanguageGen#srng} field, and maxChars, which means the sentence length
4809         * will be limited only by maxWords and the length of words produced.
4810         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4811         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4812         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4813         * @param midPunctuation an array of Strings that can be used immediately after words in the middle of sentences, like "," or ";"
4814         * @param endPunctuation an array of Strings that can end a sentence, like ".", "?", or "..."
4815         * @param midPunctuationFrequency the probability that two words will be separated by a String from midPunctuation, between 0.0 and 1.0
4816         */
4817        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, int minWords, int maxWords, String[] midPunctuation,
4818                            String[] endPunctuation, double midPunctuationFrequency)
4819        {
4820            this(language, FakeLanguageGen.srng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation,
4821                    midPunctuationFrequency, -1);
4822        }
4823        /**
4824         * Builds a SentenceForm with all fields specified except for {@link #rng}, which will be made based on
4825         * FakeLanguageGen's static {@link FakeLanguageGen#srng} field.
4826         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4827         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4828         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4829         * @param midPunctuation an array of Strings that can be used immediately after words in the middle of sentences, like "," or ";"
4830         * @param endPunctuation an array of Strings that can end a sentence, like ".", "?", or "..."
4831         * @param midPunctuationFrequency the probability that two words will be separated by a String from midPunctuation, between 0.0 and 1.0
4832         * @param maxChars the maximum number of chars to use in a sentence, or -1 for no hard limit
4833         */
4834        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, int minWords, int maxWords, String[] midPunctuation,
4835                            String[] endPunctuation, double midPunctuationFrequency, int maxChars)
4836        {
4837            this(language, FakeLanguageGen.srng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation,
4838                    midPunctuationFrequency, maxChars);
4839        }
4840
4841        /**
4842         * Builds a SentenceForm with all fields specified; each value is referenced directly except for {@code rng},
4843         * which will not change or be directly referenced (a new StatefulRNG will be used with the same state value).
4844         * Note that the StatefulRandomness used by this class' rng field will always be LinnormRNG, even if the given
4845         * rng parameter used a different StatefulRandomness implementation.
4846         * @param language A FakeLanguageGen to use to generate words
4847         * @param rng a StatefulRNG that will not be directly referenced; the state will be copied into a new StatefulRNG
4848         * @param minWords minimum words per sentence
4849         * @param maxWords maximum words per sentence
4850         * @param midPunctuation an array of Strings that can be used immediately after words in the middle of sentences, like "," or ";"
4851         * @param endPunctuation an array of Strings that can end a sentence, like ".", "?", or "..."
4852         * @param midPunctuationFrequency the probability that two words will be separated by a String from midPunctuation, between 0.0 and 1.0
4853         * @param maxChars the maximum number of chars to use in a sentence, or -1 for no hard limit
4854         */
4855        public SentenceForm(FakeLanguageGen language, StatefulRNG rng, int minWords, int maxWords,
4856                            String[] midPunctuation, String[] endPunctuation,
4857                            double midPunctuationFrequency, int maxChars)
4858        {
4859            this.language = language;
4860            this.rng = new StatefulRNG(rng.getState());
4861            this.minWords = minWords;
4862            this.maxWords = maxWords;
4863            this.midPunctuation = midPunctuation;
4864            this.endPunctuation = endPunctuation;
4865            this.midPunctuationFrequency = midPunctuationFrequency;
4866            this.maxChars = maxChars;
4867        }
4868        public String sentence()
4869        {
4870            return language.sentence(rng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation,
4871                    midPunctuationFrequency, maxChars);
4872        }
4873
4874        public String serializeToString() {
4875            return language.serializeToString() + '℘' +
4876                    rng.getState() + '℘' +
4877                    minWords + '℘' +
4878                    maxWords + '℘' +
4879                    StringKit.join("ℙ", midPunctuation) + '℘' +
4880                    StringKit.join("ℙ", endPunctuation) + '℘' +
4881                    NumberTools.doubleToLongBits(midPunctuationFrequency) + '℘' +
4882                    maxChars;
4883        }
4884        public static SentenceForm deserializeFromString(String ser)
4885        {
4886            int gap = ser.indexOf('℘');
4887            FakeLanguageGen lang = FakeLanguageGen.deserializeFromString(ser.substring(0, gap));
4888            StatefulRNG rng = new StatefulRNG(
4889                    StringKit.longFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)));
4890            int minWords = StringKit.intFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1));
4891            int maxWords = StringKit.intFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1));
4892            String[] midPunctuation =
4893                    StringKit.split(ser.substring(gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)), "ℙ");
4894            String[] endPunctuation =
4895                    StringKit.split(ser.substring(gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)), "ℙ");
4896            double midFreq = NumberTools.longBitsToDouble(StringKit.longFromDec(ser,gap + 1, gap = ser.indexOf('℘', gap + 1)));
4897            int maxChars = StringKit.intFromDec(ser,gap + 1, ser.length());
4898            return new SentenceForm(lang, rng, minWords, maxWords, midPunctuation, endPunctuation, midFreq, maxChars);
4899        }
4900    }
4901}
